perform better on using BEI passives for translating unfavourable content and
avoid using it for neutral and favourable content. Also, in NLLB-600M, which is
a multilingual model, this knowledge of semantic prosody can be transferred
from English-Chinese translation to other language pairs, such as
Spanish-Chinese.

### [108] [AutoRubric-R1V: Rubric-Based Generative Rewards for Faithful Multimodal Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.14738)

with verifiable rewards (RLVR) often leads to spurious reasoning since only the

### [109] [Pluto: A Benchmark for Evaluating Efficiency of LLM-generated Hardware Code](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.14756)
*Manar Abdelatty,Maryam Nouh,Jacob K. Rosenstein,Sherief Reda*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: Pluto 提供一个面向 Verilog 的基准和评估框架，专注于功能正确性之外的综合效率（面积、时延、功耗）评估。含114个问题、自检测试平台和多种帕累托最优参考实现；LLMs 在功能正确性方面表现良好，但综合效率明显落后专家实现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基准多聚焦功能正确性，缺乏对综合效率的全面评估；需要一个能同时评估功能正确性和综合指标的基准来推动面向硬件的LLM研究。

Method: 构建 Pluto 基准与评估框架，提供114个问题、带自检测试平台、多个帕累托最优参考实现；通过对比功能正确性（pass@1）与综合指标（面积/时延/功耗的效用/eff@1）来评估LLM生成的Verilog设计。

Result: LLMs 在功能正确性方面达到高水平（pass@1 78.3%），但综合效率落后于专家实现：面积效率63.8%、时延效率65.9%、功耗效率64.0%（eff@1）。

Conclusion: 需要如 Pluto 这类以效率为导向的评估框架来推动面向硬件的LLM研究进步；未来工作可聚焦提升综合指标的优化能力、扩展测试用例与参考实现、完善自检测试平台。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) are increasingly used to automate hardware
design tasks, including the generation of Verilog code. While early benchmarks
focus primarily on functional correctness, efficient hardware design demands
additional optimization for synthesis metrics such as area, delay, and power.
Existing benchmarks fall short in evaluating these aspects comprehensively:
they often lack optimized baselines or testbenches for verification. To address
these gaps, we present Pluto, a benchmark and evaluation framework designed to
assess the efficiency of LLM-generated Verilog designs. Pluto presents a
comprehensive evaluation set of 114 problems with self-checking testbenches and
multiple Pareto-optimal reference implementations. Experimental results show
that state-of-the-art LLMs can achieve high functional correctness, reaching
78.3\% at pass@1, but their synthesis efficiency still lags behind
expert-crafted implementations, with area efficiency of 63.8\%, delay
efficiency of 65.9\%, and power efficiency of 64.0\% at eff@1. This highlights
the need for efficiency-aware evaluation frameworks such as Pluto to drive
progress in hardware-focused LLM research.

### [110] [COIG-Writer: A High-Quality Dataset for Chinese Creative Writing with Thought Processes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.14763)
*Yunwen Li,Shuangshuang Ying,Xingwei Qu,Xin Li,Sheng Jin,Minghao Liu,Zhoufutu Wen,Tianyu Zheng,Xeron Du,Qiguang Chen,Jiajun Shi,Wangchunshu Zhou,Jiazhan Feng,Wanjun Zhong,Libo Qin,Stephen Huang,Wanxiang Che,Chenghua Lin,Eli Zhang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: COIG-Writer 是一个面向中文创作的数据集，提供可逆推理提示、创作过程记录与最终文本，揭示过程监督与语言 grounding 的协同作用，并指出在中文创作中的跨语言限制与词汇多样性悖论。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决非英语场景中大语言模型在创造性写作方面的不足，提供含有过程级监督的高质量中文创作数据集以提升稳定性、可解释性与跨语言研究的能力。

Method: 构建 1,665 条三元组的 COIG-Writer，覆盖 51 种体裁；每条包含：(1) 可逆推理提示、(2) 详细创作推理过程、(3) 最终文本。通过系统性实验识别两组件模型：叙事逻辑（由过程监督提供）和语言表达（由通用数据维持），并通过调整创意样本与一般样本的比例来评估对创作质量与胜率的影响。

Result: 实验结果显示，最优比率为创意样本与一般样本之比为 1:12；当比例下降时胜率从 62.75% 下降到 35.78%（稳定阈值下的趋势）。另外，创作能力在中英文之间存在显著的跨语言差异（Chinese vs English，约 89.26 个百分点的差距），且词汇多样性与创作质量呈逆相关关系（TTR 悖论），表明更高的多样性可能弥补逻辑不足。

Conclusion: 创作卓越源于逻辑支架与语言 grounding 的协同，单独的推理能力无法替代语言能力；该数据集有助于理解中文创作特性并推动基于过程监督的模型改进。

Abstract: Large language models exhibit systematic deficiencies in creative writing,
particularly in non-English contexts where training data is scarce and lacks
process-level supervision. We present COIG-Writer, a novel Chinese creative
writing dataset that captures both diverse outputs and their underlying thought
processes through systematic reverse-engineering of high-quality texts. Unlike
existing datasets that provide only input-output pairs, COIG-Writer comprises
1,665 meticulously curated triplets spanning 51 genres, each containing: (1) a
reverse-engineered prompt, (2) detailed creative reasoning documenting
decision-making processes, and (3) the final text. Through comprehensive
experiments, we identify a two-component model of creative writing: narrative
logic (provided by process supervision) and linguistic expression (maintained
by general-purpose data). Our findings reveal three critical insights: (1)
Process supervision is highly effective but requires stabilization with general
data. A ratio of at least one creative sample to twelve general samples is
needed to achieve optimal performance; below this threshold, the win rate
progressively degrades (from 62.75% down to 35.78%)., (2) creative capabilities
are culturally-bound with no cross-lingual transfer (89.26pp gap between
Chinese and English performance), and (3) lexical diversity inversely
correlates with creative quality (TTR paradox), suggesting high diversity
signals compensatory behavior for logical deficiencies. These findings
establish that creative excellence emerges from the interaction between logical
scaffolding and linguistic grounding, analogous to how mathematical reasoning
enhances but cannot replace linguistic competence in foundation models.

### [111] [Finding Answers in Thought Matters: Revisiting Evaluation on Large Language Models with Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.14773)
*Hwiyeol Jo,Joosung Lee,Jaehone Lee,Sang-Woo Lee,Joonsuk Park,Kang Min Yoo*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 提出“答案再生成”框架，通过再进行一次模型推理并在输出前置“Answer:”来生成中间答案，从而在最终提取阶段与提取规则无关，提高对推理型模型评估的鲁棒性，以及在一般数学题和开放式问答中的应用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有评估往往基于选项的概率来判定答案，或依赖特定的答案提取规则，推理型模型的最终输出很容易被提取方式影响，导致评估结果不稳定。

Method: 新增一个推理步骤：在原始输入和输出的基础上进行一次额外推理，输出前加上“Answer: ”，对 regenerated 输出进行最终答案抽取，使提取规则不敏感。

Result: 在一般数学题与开放式问答任务上，展示了性能提升与鲁棒性增强，减少对具体提取规则的依赖。

Conclusion: 该框架可为模型评估提供更可靠的结果，促进对推理能力与生成质量的更公平比较。

Abstract: Evaluating generative models, such as large language models (LLMs), commonly
involves question-answering tasks where the final answer is selected based on
probability of answer choices. On the other hand, for models requiring
reasoning, the method of answer extraction plays a critical role. Our research
reveals that the performance of reasoning models and their final answer
distributions are highly sensitive to the answer extraction algorithm employed.
In order to mitigate this, we propose a basic framework: Answer Regeneration.
The method uses an additional model inference, providing the prior input and
output prefaced by the prompt "Answer:". The final answer is then selected or
extracted from the regenerated output. We show that this
extraction-rule-agnostic approach exhibits improved performance and enhanced
robustness. Furthermore, we have applied this framework to general math
problems and open-ended question answering tasks. Our analysis and this
framework could offer a more reliable results for model evaluation.

### [112] [Rewiring Experts on the Fly:Continuous Rerouting for Better Online Adaptation in Mixture-of-Expert models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.14853)
*Guinan Su,Yanwu Yang,Li Shen,Lu Yin,Shiwei Liu,Jonas Geiping*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 提出一种数据无关的在线测试时自适应框架，用于MoE路由的自适应优化：在生成过程中通过自监督微调路由逻辑，使用轻量级的添加向量仅更新特定层的路由 logits，无需外部数据，提升推理阶段的推理能力与鲁棒性（如 HumanEval 5.5% 提升，DeepSeek-V2-Lite 6% 平均提升）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: MoE通过稀疏路由实现高效扩展，但遇到部署阶段的分布漂移时，路由决策往往不理想。现有的测试时自适应方法多针对密集模型且需要外部数据，难以直接应用到MoE结构。需要一种不依赖外部数据、在线、数据无关的路由自适应方法以提升MoE在实际分布变化中的鲁棒性与性能。

Method: 提出两阶段循环：预填阶段（prefill）和定期自适应阶段。利用已生成序列进行自监督，在线优化模型的路由决策；通过轻量级的附加向量来更新仅在选定层中的路由 logits，保持计算开销低且避免过度自适应。最终在生成文本时应用修改后的路由，直至下一次自适应。该方法具备即插即用属性，能够与现有的测试时扩展技术兼容。

Result: 在具有挑战性的推理任务上显示稳定性能提升；具体现象包括对人类评测任务的提升（如 HumanEval +5.5%（在 OL-MoE 设置下））以及与自一致性（Self-Consistency）结合时在 DeepSeek-V2-Lite 上实现的平均6%增益。

Conclusion: 方法具备数据无关、在线、轻量且可插拔的特性，适用于MoE架构并可与现有测试时扩展技术协同工作，有望缓解部署阶段的分布漂移带来的路由劣化问题。潜在局限包括自监督信号的有效性依赖、对路由器结构的特定假设、以及在不同MoE实现中的泛化能力，需通过更广泛的任务和模型设置进行验证。

Abstract: Mixture-of-Experts (MoE) models achieve efficient scaling through sparse
expert activation, but often suffer from suboptimal routing decisions due to
distribution shifts in deployment. While existing test-time adaptation methods
could potentially address these issues, they primarily focus on dense models
and require access to external data, limiting their practical applicability to
MoE architectures. However, we find that, instead of relying on reference data,
we can optimize MoE expert selection on-the-fly based only on input context. As
such, we propose \textit{a data-free, online test-time framework} that
continuously adapts MoE routing decisions during text generation without
external supervision or data. Our method cycles between two phases: During the
prefill stage, and later in regular intervals, we optimize the routing
decisions of the model using self-supervision based on the already generated
sequence. Then, we generate text as normal, maintaining the modified router
until the next adaption. We implement this through lightweight additive vectors
that only update router logits in selected layers, maintaining computational
efficiency while preventing over-adaptation. The experimental results show
consistent performance gains on challenging reasoning tasks while maintaining
robustness to context shifts. For example, our method achieves a 5.5\%
improvement on HumanEval with OLMoE. Furthermore, owing to its plug-and-play
property, our method naturally complements existing test-time scaling
techniques, e.g., achieving 6\% average gains when incorporated with
self-consistency on DeepSeek-V2-Lite.

### [113] [Midtraining Bridges Pretraining and Posttraining Distributions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.14865)
*Emmy Liu,Graham Neubig,Chenyan Xiong*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: Midtraining (在预训练后期混入高质量数据) 能作为一种领域自适应技术，特别在数学和代码领域，显著降低预训练与后续微调之间的差异带来的遗忘，优于继续预训练；早期引入专业数据比调整混入比重更有效。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管midtraining在实践中流行，但缺乏系统理解。本研究通过受控实验探索其在从头预训练并在不同领域进行监督微调的语言模型上的效果，关注其为何有效及适用条件。

Method: 对从头预训练的语言模型，结合不同领域的监督微调数据，进行系统性实验；使用代码领域的midtraining作为案例，分析midtraining起始时间、数据混入权重的消融；比较midtraining与继续预训练在在域验证损失和微调后数据遗忘方面的差异。

Result: 在数学与代码领域，midtraining显著缩小了预训练与后续训练之间的语法/结构差距，且在微调后对内在数据的遗忘更少；相对继续预训练，midtraining在在域验证损失和微调后数据遗忘方面表现更优；起始时间的影响大于混入权重，提前引入专业数据往往带来更大益处，同时也更好地保护通用语言建模能力。

Conclusion: 将midtraining视为一种领域自适应技术，相较于继续预训练能通过降低遗忘提升整体性能，尤其在math/code等对结构差异敏感的领域。

Abstract: Recently, many language models have been pretrained with a "midtraining"
phase, in which higher quality, often instruction-formatted data, is mixed in
at the end of pretraining. Despite the popularity of this practice, there is
little scientific understanding of this phase of model training or why it is
effective. In this work, we conduct the first systematic investigation of
midtraining through controlled experiments with language models pretrained from
scratch and fine-tuned on supervised finetuning datasets in different domains.
We find that when compared after supervised fine-tuning, the effectiveness of
midtraining is highest in the math and code domains, where midtraining can best
reduce the syntactic gap between pretraining and posttraining data. In these
cases, midtraining consistently outperforms continued pretraining in both
in-domain validation loss as well as pretraining data forgetting after
posttraining. We conduct ablations on the starting time of the midtraining
phase and mixture weights of the midtraining data, using code midtraining as a
case study, and find that timing has a greater impact than mixture weights,
with earlier introduction of specialized data, yielding greater benefits
in-domain as well as preserving general language modeling better. These
findings establish midtraining as a domain adaptation technique that compared
to continued pretraining yields better performance through reduced forgetting.

### [114] [From Loop Nests to Silicon: Mapping AI Workloads onto AMD NPUs with MLIR-AIR](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.14871)
*Erwei Wang,Samuel Bayliss,Andra Bisca,Zachary Blair,Sangeeta Chowdhary,Kristof Denolf,Jeff Fifield,Brandon Freiberger,Erika Hunhoff,Phil James-Roxby,Jack Lo,Joseph Melber,Stephen Neuendorffer,Eddie Richter,Andre Rosti,Javier Setoain,Gagandeep Singh,Endri Taka,Pranathi Vasireddy,Zhewen Yu,Niansong Zhang,Jinming Zhuang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: MLIR-AIR 是一个基于 MLIR 的新型编译堆栈，定义 AIR 交易以显式控制空间计算和数据布局，能把高层工作负载映射到像 AMD NPUs 这样的细粒度空间架构，且在矩阵乘法和多头注意力上表现出具竞争力的性能与可表达性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前通用编译器倾向于抽象化并隐藏并行性、数据位置与同步，导致在需细粒度控制的数据移动和执行顺序的现代空间架构上效率受限。需要显式的机制来编排计算与数据流以充分发挥硬件潜力。

Method: 提出 AIR dialect，提供异步和层次化操作的结构化表示，覆盖 compute 与 memory 资源；通过编译器管理的调度实现空间调度、区域级分布和计算与通信的重叠；在 MLIR-AIR 框架中实现并通过矩阵乘法和多头注意力案例进行验证。

Result: 在矩阵乘法中达到最高 78.7% 的计算效率，生成的实现接近最先进的手写优化（基于低层 MLIR-AIE 框架）。在多头注意力方面，AIR 接口支持融合实现，代码量约 150 行即可表达复杂 workload，并高效映射到空间硬件。

Conclusion: MLIR-AIR 将高层结构化控制流转化为可高效利用 NPU 的空间程序，利用异步执行、切块和通信重叠实现编译器管理的调度，减少对 ad-hoc 运行时协调或人工调度的依赖。

Abstract: General-purpose compilers abstract away parallelism, locality, and
synchronization, limiting their effectiveness on modern spatial architectures.
As modern computing architectures increasingly rely on fine-grained control
over data movement, execution order, and compute placement for performance,
compiler infrastructure must provide explicit mechanisms for orchestrating
compute and data to fully exploit such architectures. We introduce MLIR-AIR, a
novel, open-source compiler stack built on MLIR that bridges the semantic gap
between high-level workloads and fine-grained spatial architectures such as
AMD's NPUs. MLIR-AIR defines the AIR dialect, which provides structured
representations for asynchronous and hierarchical operations across compute and
memory resources. AIR primitives allow the compiler to orchestrate spatial
scheduling, distribute computation across hardware regions, and overlap
communication with computation without relying on ad hoc runtime coordination
or manual scheduling. We demonstrate MLIR-AIR's capabilities through two case
studies: matrix multiplication and the multi-head attention block from the
LLaMA 2 model. For matrix multiplication, MLIR-AIR achieves up to 78.7% compute
efficiency and generates implementations with performance almost identical to
state-of-the-art, hand-optimized matrix multiplication written using the
lower-level, close-to-metal MLIR-AIE framework. For multi-head attention, we
demonstrate that the AIR interface supports fused implementations using
approximately 150 lines of code, enabling tractable expression of complex
workloads with efficient mapping to spatial hardware. MLIR-AIR transforms
high-level structured control flow into spatial programs that efficiently
utilize the compute fabric and memory hierarchy of an NPU, leveraging
asynchronous execution, tiling, and communication overlap through
compiler-managed scheduling.

</details>


### [115] [Harmonizing Diverse Models: A Layer-wise Merging Strategy for Consistent Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.14915)
*Xujun Peng,Anoop Kumar,Jingyu Wu,Parker Glenn,Daben Liu*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLMs在对等语义输入下输出不一致；缺乏专注于一致性的训练数据；现有微调方法难以显著提升输出一致性。为了提升工业化RAG系统的可靠性，需要提升模型在语义等价输入上的输出一致性并有效融合专用知识。

Method: 1) 通过系统化的合成数据生成覆盖不同语义等价输入；2) 采用三元组损失优化嵌入空间，使语义等价输入的表示更紧凑且相似；3) 提出层级模型融合（layer-wise model merging），利用来自中间层激活的“一致性权重”将专用模型的知识以受控方式整合到主模型中，使输出更加一致。

Result: 融合后的模型显著提升输出一致性，相对于基线的响应相似度提升约47.5%，显示出在工业RAG系统中提升可靠性的可行性。

Conclusion: 该方法为提升RAG系统输出一致性提供了一个可操作的路径：通过合成数据、嵌入级对齐和分层融合三方面协同作用，显著增强语义等价输入下的输出一致性，具有较强的实际应用潜力与扩展性。未来可进一步探讨对抗性评估、跨任务的一致性以及更高效的融合策略。

Abstract: Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG) systems leverage Large Language Models
(LLMs) to generate accurate and reliable responses that are grounded in
retrieved context. However, LLMs often generate inconsistent outputs for
semantically equivalent inputs, a problem compounded by the scarcity of
consistency-focused training data and the limitations of current fine-tuning
techniques in enhancing output consistency. We propose a new approach combining
systematic synthetic data generation, triplet loss for better embeddings, and a
novel layer-wise model merging approach. Using consistency-aware weights
derived from intermediate layer activations, our method effectively integrates
knowledge from specialized models. Experimental results how that our merged
model significantly enhances output consistency, achieving a ~47.5\%
improvement in response similarity over the baseline, thus offering a practical

### [116] [Predicting Task Performance with Context-aware Scaling Laws](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.14919)
*Kyle Montgomery,David Park,Jianhong Tu,Michael Bendersky,Beliz Gunel,Dawn Song,Chenguang Wang*

Abstract: Scaling laws have transformed our understanding of large language models by
linking upstream metrics like cross-entropy loss to design factors such as
model size, training data, and compute. However, these conventional laws fail
to capture downstream task performance, where context plays a critical role. In
this work, we propose a straightforward, interpretable framework that jointly
models downstream performance as a function of the training compute and the
provided context. We empirically validate our framework by fitting it on the
observed downstream performance of extended-context variants of Llama-2-7B and
Llama-2-13B across 65,500 unique instances spanning three tasks: arithmetic
reasoning, common sense reasoning, and machine translation. Our results
demonstrate that our framework accurately models in-distribution downstream
performance, generalizes across three orders of magnitude in training compute,
and reliably extrapolates performance as the amount of context increases. These
findings offer valuable insights into the interplay between training compute
and context utilization, providing guidance for designing more efficient
long-context LLMs for diverse downstream tasks. Our code is available at
https://github.com/wang-research-lab/context-scaling.

### [117] [AI-Powered Early Diagnosis of Mental Health Disorders from Real-World Clinical Conversations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.14937)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 精神疾病全球负担沉重，诊断常被低估或误诊，原因包括主观评估、资源不足、污名与认知不足等。需开发可扩展、情境感知的诊断工具，特别是在初级保健中以实现早期检测和干预。

Method: 在553份真实世界半结构化访谈数据上，比较多种模型：零-shot提示的GPT-4.1 Mini、MetaLLaMA；对RoBERTa进行LoRA微调。诊断标签覆盖抑郁发作、焦虑、PTSD；评估准确率、召回率等指标。

Result: 各模型在诊断类别上均达到80%以上的准确率，PTSD表现尤佳，准确率可达89%、召回率达98%；更短的上下文/聚焦段可提升召回；LoRA低秩（如8、16）微调在保持竞争力的同时提高效率。总体上，LLM驱动模型优于传统自我报告筛查工具。

Conclusion: LLM驱动的精神健康筛查具备落地潜力，能在低资源或高污名环境中支持早期诊断与干预，并可逐步融入现实世界临床工作流。

Abstract: Mental health disorders remain among the leading cause of disability
worldwide, yet conditions such as depression, anxiety, and Post-Traumatic
Stress Disorder (PTSD) are frequently underdiagnosed or misdiagnosed due to
subjective assessments, limited clinical resources, and stigma and low
awareness. In primary care settings, studies show that providers misidentify
depression or anxiety in over 60% of cases, highlighting the urgent need for
scalable, accessible, and context-aware diagnostic tools that can support early
detection and intervention. In this study, we evaluate the effectiveness of
machine learning models for mental health screening using a unique dataset of
553 real-world, semistructured interviews, each paried with ground-truth
diagnoses for major depressive episodes (MDE), anxiety disorders, and PTSD. We
benchmark multiple model classes, including zero-shot prompting with GPT-4.1
Mini and MetaLLaMA, as well as fine-tuned RoBERTa models using LowRank
Adaptation (LoRA). Our models achieve over 80% accuracy across diagnostic
categories, with especially strongperformance on PTSD (up to 89% accuracy and
98% recall). We also find that using shorter context, focused context segments
improves recall, suggesting that focused narrative cues enhance detection
sensitivity. LoRA fine-tuning proves both efficient and effective, with
lower-rank configurations (e.g., rank 8 and 16) maintaining competitive
performance across evaluation metrics. Our results demonstrate that LLM-based
models can offer substantial improvements over traditional self-report
screening tools, providing a path toward low-barrier, AI-powerd early
diagnosis. This work lays the groundwork for integrating machine learning into
real-world clinical workflows, particularly in low-resource or high-stigma
environments where access to timely mental health care is most limited.

</details>


### [118] [LaSeR: Reinforcement Learning with Last-Token Self-Rewarding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.14943)
*Wenkai Yang,Weijie Liu,Ruobing Xie,Yiju Guo,Lulu Wu,Saiyong Yang,Yankai Lin*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 提出 LaSeR，一种用最后一个 token 的自奖励分数来近似 RLVR 的真推理奖励的无缝训练框架，并在训练和推理阶段利用这一分数来实现自验证与推理的联合优化，从而提高推理性能和推理时推理能力的可扩展性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决测试时缺乏验证信号的问题；现有方法需要用两份提示模板进行自我验证，效率低下；寻找一个闭式解把自我验证的 RL 目标简化，同时保留推理与自我验证能力。

Method: 理论推导出 RL 目标的闭式解：真推理奖励等于最后一个 token 的自奖励分数，即当前策略模型对最后 token 之后的下一个 token 的对数概率与预先设定常数之差，乘以 KL 系数。基于此，提出 LaSeR：在原 RLVR 损失上增加一个 MSE 损失，使最后 token 的自奖励分数与 verifier 基于推理的奖励对齐；训练和推理阶段均可使用这些分数，且只需再做一次 token 推断即可获得。实验表明方法提升推理性能并赋予模型强自奖励能力，从而提升推理推断时的可扩展性。

Result: 在推理表征和自奖励能力方面有显著提升；训练时对自奖励分数的对齐提高了推理质量，推理时增加的一个 token 推断成本很小；提升了推理时的扩展性。

Conclusion: LaSeR 提供一个高效的 RLVR 框架，通过最后一个 token 的自奖励分数来近似真奖励，简化了训练流程并在推理阶段保持性能提升，适用于提升 LLM 的推理与自验证能力。

Abstract: Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) has recently emerged as
a core paradigm for enhancing the reasoning capabilities of Large Language
Models (LLMs). To address the lack of verification signals at test time, prior
studies incorporate the training of model's self-verification capability into
the standard RLVR process, thereby unifying reasoning and verification
capabilities within a single LLM. However, previous practice requires the LLM
to sequentially generate solutions and self-verifications using two separate
prompt templates, which significantly reduces efficiency. In this work, we
theoretically reveal that the closed-form solution to the RL objective of
self-verification can be reduced to a remarkably simple form: the true
reasoning reward of a solution is equal to its last-token self-rewarding score,
which is computed as the difference between the policy model's next-token
log-probability assigned to any pre-specified token at the solution's last
token and a pre-calculated constant, scaled by the KL coefficient. Based on
this insight, we propose LaSeR (Reinforcement Learning with Last-Token
Self-Rewarding), an algorithm that simply augments the original RLVR loss with
a MSE loss that aligns the last-token self-rewarding scores with verifier-based
reasoning rewards, jointly optimizing the reasoning and self-rewarding
capabilities of LLMs. The optimized self-rewarding scores can be utilized in
both training and testing to enhance model performance. Notably, our algorithm
derives these scores from the predicted next-token probability distribution of
the last token immediately after generation, incurring only the minimal extra
cost of one additional token inference. Experiments show that our method not
only improves the model's reasoning performance but also equips it with
remarkable self-rewarding capability, thereby boosting its inference-time
scaling performance.

</details>

*Yuxing Lu,Xukai Zhao,J. Ben Tamo,Micky C. Nnamdi,Rui Peng,Shuang Zeng,Xingyu Hu,Jinzhuo Wang,May D. Wang*

Method: 基于权威公开资源整理数据集，评估 25 个开源与闭源 LLM 在五项能力上的表现，并探索通过检索增强提升 grounding 的效果；关注长尾代谢物注释稀疏带来的影响。

Result: 在文本生成任务上模型表现不俗；跨数据库标识符 grounding 仍具挑战，检索增强未显著提升；长尾代谢物注释稀疏导致性能下降。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) have demonstrated remarkable capabilities on

### [120] [DialectGen: Benchmarking and Improving Dialect Robustness in Multimodal Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.14949)
*Yu Zhou,Sohyun An,Haikang Deng,Da Yin,Clark Peng,Cho-Jui Hsieh,Kai-Wei Chang,Nanyun Peng*

TL;DR: 提出并评估一个跨六种英语方言的大规模基准，揭示当前多模态生成模型在方言提示下的显著下降，并给出一种通用的基于编码器的缓解策略，能在不损害SAE的前提下显著提升方言鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 构建覆盖六种英语方言的大规模基准，招募方言说话者，收集并核验超过4200条提示，并在17个图像/视频生成模型上进行自动与人工评估。基于此提出一种基于编码器的缓解策略，使模型能够识别并利用方言特征，同时尽量保持SAE性能。对Stable Diffusion 1.5等模型进行实验，验证该方法在五种方言上将性能提升至与SAE相当，并对SAE几乎无成本。

Conclusion: 所提出的编码器级缓解策略为多模态生成模型在方言鲁棒性上的挑战提供了一个可通用且高效的解决方案，能在不牺牲SAE的前提下显著提升方言输入的理解和生成质量，适用于包括图像与视频生成在内的多模态任务。

Abstract: Contact languages like English exhibit rich regional variations in the form

produce content given dialectal textual input? In this work, we study this
question by constructing a new large-scale benchmark spanning six common
English dialects. We work with dialect speakers to collect and verify over 4200
unique prompts and evaluate on 17 image and video generative models. Our
automatic and human evaluation results show that current state-of-the-art
multimodal generative models exhibit 32.26% to 48.17% performance degradation

such as fine-tuning and prompt rewriting can only improve dialect performance
by small margins (< 7%), while potentially incurring significant performance

performance. Experiments on models such as Stable Diffusion 1.5 show that our

par with SAE (+34.4%), while incurring near zero cost to SAE performance.

### [121] [Information Gain-based Policy Optimization: A Simple and Effective Approach for Multi-Turn LLM Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.14967)
*Guoqing Wang,Sunhao Dai,Guangze Ye,Zeyu Gan,Wei Yao,Yong Deng,Xiaofeng Wu,Zhenzhe Ying*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: IGPO 提出一种基于信息增益的策略优化框架，为多轮对话式强化学习中的LLM代理提供密集的内在奖励。通过把每一轮视为逐步获取关于真相的信息的过程，将回报定义为正确回答概率的边际提升，并将内在奖励与结果奖励结合，改善学习信号的密度，缓解奖励稀疏和信用分配难题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多轮交互中使用工具的LLM强化学习常受奖励稀疏困扰，尤其在长轨迹下存在优势崩溃和难以进行细粒度信用分配的问题。需要更密集、内在的监督信号来提升学习效率和效果。

Method: 把每一轮交互建模为获取关于Ground Truth的信息的增量过程；将轮级奖励定义为模型对正确答案概率的边际提升；内在奖励直接来自模型自身的信念更新，避免外部奖励模型和昂贵的Monte Carlo估计；将轮级内在奖励与结果层面的监督结合，形成密集的奖励轨迹。

Result: 在多轮场景下的内域和外域基准上，IGPO持续优于强基线，表现为更高的正确性和更好的样本效率。实验覆盖多种数据域，显示方法的鲁棒性与泛化性。

Conclusion: IGPO提供一个简单而有效的RL框架，利用信息增益驱动的轮级信号缓解奖励稀疏与信用分配问题，改善多轮LLM Agent的学习效果和效率。

Abstract: Large language model (LLM)-based agents are increasingly trained with
reinforcement learning (RL) to enhance their ability to interact with external
environments through tool use, particularly in search-based settings that
require multi-turn reasoning and knowledge acquisition. However, existing
approaches typically rely on outcome-based rewards that are only provided at
the final answer. This reward sparsity becomes particularly problematic in
multi-turn settings, where long trajectories exacerbate two critical issues:
(i) advantage collapse, where all rollouts receive identical rewards and
provide no useful learning signals, and (ii) lack of fine-grained credit
assignment, where dependencies between turns are obscured, especially in
long-horizon tasks. In this paper, we propose Information Gain-based Policy
Optimization (IGPO), a simple yet effective RL framework that provides dense
and intrinsic supervision for multi-turn agent training. IGPO models each
interaction turn as an incremental process of acquiring information about the
ground truth, and defines turn-level rewards as the marginal increase in the
policy's probability of producing the correct answer. Unlike prior
process-level reward approaches that depend on external reward models or costly
Monte Carlo estimation, IGPO derives intrinsic rewards directly from the
model's own belief updates. These intrinsic turn-level rewards are combined
with outcome-level supervision to form dense reward trajectories. Extensive
experiments on both in-domain and out-of-domain benchmarks demonstrate that
IGPO consistently outperforms strong baselines in multi-turn scenarios,
achieving higher accuracy and improved sample efficiency.

</details>

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 获取大规模、多样化的 UI 轨迹以提升数字代理在现实任务中的泛化能力，但真实数据采集成本高（人工标注、基础设施、工程实现等）。

Method: 构建一个数字世界仿真器以生成多样化的 UI 状态，设计引导式 rollout 以实现连贯探索，并实现一个轨迹包装器来产出高质量、多样化的训练轨迹。同时提出 UI-Simulator-Grow 作为有针对性的扩展策略，优先覆盖高影响任务并合成信息丰富的轨迹变体。

Result: 在 WebArena 和 AndroidWorld 上，UI-Simulator 的表现等同或优于在真实 UI 上训练的开源代理，同时鲁棒性显著提升；即使教师模型较弱。UI-Simulator-Grow 的性能可与 Llama-3-70B-Instruct 相当，且仅需基于 Llama-3-8B-Instruct 的模型。

Conclusion: 有针对性的合成扩展可以持续且高效地提升数字代理的性能，展示了通过大规模合成数据提升 UI 任务代理能力的潜力。

Abstract: Digital agents require diverse, large-scale UI trajectories to generalize

both human annotation, infra and engineering perspectives. To this end, we
introduce $\textbf{UI-Simulator}$, a scalable paradigm that generates
structured UI states and transitions to synthesize training trajectories at
scale. Our paradigm integrates a digital world simulator for diverse UI states,
a guided rollout process for coherent exploration, and a trajectory wrapper
that produces high-quality and diverse trajectories for agent training. We
further propose $\textbf{UI-Simulator-Grow}$, a targeted scaling strategy that
enables more rapid and data-efficient scaling by prioritizing high-impact tasks
and synthesizes informative trajectory variants. Experiments on WebArena and
AndroidWorld show that UI-Simulator rivals or surpasses open-source agents
trained on real UIs with significantly better robustness, despite using weaker

### [123] [TokDrift: When LLM Speaks in Subwords but Code Speaks in Grammar](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.14972)
*Yinxi Li,Yuntian Deng,Pengyu Nie*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 语义不变的代码变体会引发代码语言模型（LLMs）在标记化上的漂移，且这种漂移源自早期嵌入阶段的分词不抓住语法边界，影响模型行为；需要引入语法感知的标记化以提升代码理解与生成的鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有子词标记器（如 BPE）在混合自然语言与代码的训练语料上统计驱动，而非语法规则，导致对语义等价的代码片段在不同格式（如空格、标识符命名）下被不同的标记化处理，进而影响模型表现的可靠性。

Method: 提出 TokDrift 框架，通过语义保持的改写规则生成仅在标记化层面不同、但语义等价的代码变体；在九个代码 LLMs（其中包括参数规模超过 30B 的模型）上评估，进行层级分析以定位问题源头，重点在早期嵌入层的分词边界和语法边界未被捕捉。

Result: 即使是微小的格式化变动也会引起模型行为的显著变化；九个模型中，该问题均有体现，且初步分析指向早期嵌入层的分词机制为根源，说明当前分词对语法边界的捕捉不足。

Conclusion: 标记化与代码语法之间的错配是影响代码理解与生成的隐性障碍，需在未来的代码 LLM 设计中采用语法感知的标记化策略，以提升鲁棒性与可靠性。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) for code rely on subword tokenizers, such as
byte-pair encoding (BPE), learned from mixed natural language text and
programming language code but driven by statistics rather than grammar. As a
result, semantically identical code snippets can be tokenized differently
depending on superficial factors such as whitespace or identifier naming. To
measure the impact of this misalignment, we introduce TokDrift, a framework
that applies semantic-preserving rewrite rules to create code variants
differing only in tokenization. Across nine code LLMs, including large ones
with over 30B parameters, even minor formatting changes can cause substantial
shifts in model behavior. Layer-wise analysis shows that the issue originates
in early embeddings, where subword segmentation fails to capture grammar token
boundaries. Our findings identify misaligned tokenization as a hidden obstacle
to reliable code understanding and generation, highlighting the need for
grammar-aware tokenization for future code LLMs.

</details>


### [124] [Attention Is All You Need for KV Cache in Diffusion LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.14973)
*Quan Nguyen-Tri,Mukul Ranjan,Zhiqiang Shen*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: Elastic-Cache：一种自适应缓存刷新策略，用于扩散式大语言模型，显著降低解码延迟并保持或提升准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有解码中对所有 token 在每一步/每层重新计算QKV，导致大量冗余，尤其浅层；需要更高效的缓存管理以提高吞吐和降低延迟。

Method: 提出 Elastic-Cache，基于三条观察：远端 MASK token的长度偏置可缓存、深度增加带来 KV 动态性、最被关注的 token 的 KV 漂移最小。通过注意力漂移测试来决定何时刷新（在最关注 token 上进行测试）以及深度感知调度来决定从哪一层开始刷新并重用浅层缓存与窗口外 MASK 缓存。训练无关、架构无关，适用于扩散式 LLM。与固定周期相比，进行自适应、层级感知的缓存更新。

Result: 在 LLaDA-Instruct、LLaDA-1.5、LLaDA-V 的数学推理和代码生成任务上实现显著加速：GSM8K 256 token：8.7×，更长序列：45.1×，HumanEval：4.8×，并在总体上保持更高准确性。此外吞吐量比现有基于置信度的方法高出 6.8×，实现了更高的实用性。

Conclusion: Elastic-Cache 提供一种训练无关、架构无关的自适应缓存方案，能在扩散式 LLMs 的解码中显著降低冗余、加速推理，同时保持或提升生成质量，便于实际部署。

Abstract: This work studies how to adaptively recompute key-value (KV) caches for
diffusion large language models (DLMs) to maximize prediction accuracy while
minimizing decoding latency. Prior methods' decoders recompute QKV for all
tokens at every denoising step and layer, despite KV states changing little
across most steps, especially in shallow layers, leading to substantial
redundancy. We make three observations: (1) distant ${\bf MASK}$ tokens
primarily act as a length-bias and can be cached block-wise beyond the active
prediction window; (2) KV dynamics increase with depth, suggesting that
selective refresh starting from deeper layers is sufficient; and (3) the
most-attended token exhibits the smallest KV drift, providing a conservative
lower bound on cache change for other tokens. Building on these, we propose
${\bf Elastic-Cache}$, a training-free, architecture-agnostic strategy that
jointly decides ${when}$ to refresh (via an attention-aware drift test on the
most-attended token) and ${where}$ to refresh (via a depth-aware schedule that
recomputes from a chosen layer onward while reusing shallow-layer caches and
off-window MASK caches). Unlike fixed-period schemes, Elastic-Cache performs
adaptive, layer-aware cache updates for diffusion LLMs, reducing redundant
computation and accelerating decoding with negligible loss in generation
quality. Experiments on LLaDA-Instruct, LLaDA-1.5, and LLaDA-V across
mathematical reasoning and code generation tasks demonstrate consistent
speedups: $8.7\times$ on GSM8K (256 tokens), $45.1\times$ on longer sequences,
and $4.8\times$ on HumanEval, while consistently maintaining higher accuracy
than the baseline. Our method achieves significantly higher throughput
($6.8\times$ on GSM8K) than existing confidence-based approaches while
preserving generation quality, enabling practical deployment of diffusion LLMs.

</details>

# cs.IR [[Back]](#toc)

### [125] [FinAI Data Assistant: LLM-based Financial Database Query Processing with the OpenAI Function Calling API](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.14162)
*Juhyeong Kim,Yejin Kim,Youngbin Lee,Hyunwoo Byun*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 一个将大语言模型与函数调用结合用于金融数据库查询的实用框架：FinAI 数据助手，通过固定参数化查询库替代文本到SQL，以提高可靠性、低延迟和成本效率。通过RQ1-3的实验，发现LLM单独在时间依赖数据上的预测存在显著误差和看前偏差，股票价格尤为明显；股票代码映射对 NASDAQ-100 准确度接近完美，对标的S&P 500 也较高；相比文本到SQL，函数调用在端到端查询中的延迟、成本和可靠性更优。讨论设计权衡、局限性与部署途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决自然语言查询金融数据库的可行性与鲁棒性难题，超越单纯的 text-to-SQL、避免对时间敏感数据的误用；通过可控、参数化查询库提升可靠性、速度与成本效益。

Method: 将LLMs与 OpenAI Function Calling API 相结合，用户请求路由到一个经过审核的参数化查询库；在价格与基本面数据上进行对比实验，回答三大研究问题（RQ1-3），与 text-to-SQL 基线进行对比。

Result: LLM 仅预测存在显著误差，且对股票价格存在看前偏差；股票代码映射对 NASDAQ-100 成分股几近完美，对 S&P 500 公司也较高；FinAI Data Assistant 相对于 text-to-SQL 基线在任务集合上实现了更低的延迟、更低的成本和更高的可靠性。

Conclusion: 基于函数调用的设计在可靠性、延迟与成本方面优于文本到SQL，具有可部署性；同时需要权衡设计取舍、指出局限性并提出未来部署路径。

Abstract: We present FinAI Data Assistant, a practical approach for natural-language
querying over financial databases that combines large language models (LLMs)
with the OpenAI Function Calling API. Rather than synthesizing complete SQL via
text-to-SQL, our system routes user requests to a small library of vetted,
parameterized queries, trading generative flexibility for reliability, low
latency, and cost efficiency. We empirically study three questions: (RQ1)
whether LLMs alone can reliably recall or extrapolate time-dependent financial
data without external retrieval; (RQ2) how well LLMs map company names to stock
ticker symbols; and (RQ3) whether function calling outperforms text-to-SQL for
end-to-end database query processing. Across controlled experiments on prices
and fundamentals, LLM-only predictions exhibit non-negligible error and show
look-ahead bias primarily for stock prices relative to model knowledge cutoffs.
Ticker-mapping accuracy is near-perfect for NASDAQ-100 constituents and high
for S\&P~500 firms. Finally, FinAI Data Assistant achieves lower latency and
cost and higher reliability than a text-to-SQL baseline on our task suite. We
discuss design trade-offs, limitations, and avenues for deployment.

</details>


### [126] [Large Scale Retrieval for the LinkedIn Feed using Causal Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.14223)
*Sudarshan Srinivasa Ramanujam,Antonio Alonso,Saurabh Kataria,Siddharth Dangi,Akhilesh Gupta,Birjodh Singh Tiwana,Manas Somaiya,Luke Simon,David Byrne,Sojeong Ha,Sen Zhou,Andrei Akterskii,Zhanglong Liu,Samira Sriram,Crescent Xiong,Zhoutao Pei,Angela Shao,Alex Li,Annie Xiao,Caitlin Kolb,Thomas Kistler,Zach Moore,Hamed Firooz*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 通过将大模型（LLaMA 3）微调为双编码器来生成用户与内容的文本嵌入，用于高吞吐、低延迟的检索，显著提升在线指标，尤其对新成员的参与度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在大规模推荐中，检索阶段需要在百百万级候选中快速筛选到少量候选，同时需与排序层良好对齐。现有方法难以同时实现高质量嵌入和低延迟在线服务。

Method: 将 LLaMA 3 微调为用户与内容的双编码器，利用纯文本输入生成嵌入，设计用于嵌入生成的提示（含对数字特征的量化编码）。构建端到端管线，优化在线低延迟部署与成本，进行离线评估和在线 A/B 测试以验证效果。

Result: 离线指标与在线 A/B 测试均显示显著提升，尤其新成员群体的参与度提高，表明高质量的推荐内容有助于留存。

Conclusion: 表明生成式语言模型可高效地用于工业级实时、高吞吐的检索任务，通过对嵌入进行对齐实现检索与排序的协同提升，同时具备低延迟、成本效益的在线服务潜力。

Abstract: In large scale recommendation systems like the LinkedIn Feed, the retrieval
stage is critical for narrowing hundreds of millions of potential candidates to
a manageable subset for ranking. LinkedIn's Feed serves suggested content from
outside of the member's network (based on the member's topical interests),
where 2000 candidates are retrieved from a pool of hundreds of millions
candidate with a latency budget of a few milliseconds and inbound QPS of
several thousand per second. This paper presents a novel retrieval approach
that fine-tunes a large causal language model (Meta's LLaMA 3) as a dual
encoder to generate high quality embeddings for both users (members) and
content (items), using only textual input. We describe the end to end pipeline,
including prompt design for embedding generation, techniques for fine-tuning at
LinkedIn's scale, and infrastructure for low latency, cost effective online
serving. We share our findings on how quantizing numerical features in the
prompt enables the information to get properly encoded in the embedding,
facilitating greater alignment between the retrieval and ranking layer. The
system was evaluated using offline metrics and an online A/B test, which showed
substantial improvements in member engagement. We observed significant gains
among newer members, who often lack strong network connections, indicating that
high-quality suggested content aids retention. This work demonstrates how
generative language models can be effectively adapted for real time, high
throughput retrieval in industrial applications.

</details>


### [127] [Synergistic Integration and Discrepancy Resolution of Contextualized Knowledge for Personalized Recommendation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.14257)
*Lingyu Mu,Hao Deng,Haibo Xing,Kaican Lin,Zhitong Zhu,Yu Zhang,Xiaoyi Zeng,Zhengxiao Liu,Zheng Lin,Jinxin Hu*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 提出 CoCo 框架，通过动态构建用户上下文知识嵌入，结合语义和行为潜在维度，实现对推荐系统中知识增强推理与个性化适配的深度融合，显著提升推荐准确性和销售额。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前基于静态模板 prompting 的方法无法同时满足用户偏好多样性和语义知识与行为特征的全面对齐，导致知识增强在推荐中的潜在能力受限。

Method: 提出一个端到端、模型无关的框架 CoCo，通过双机制实现知识嵌入的自适应融合。动态构建用户特定上下文知识嵌入，结合自适应知识融合与矛盾消解模块，将语义知识与行为潜在维度进行深度整合。

Result: 在多個基准数据集与一个企业级电商平台上，最高实现 8.58% 的推荐准确性提升；在生产广告系统部署后实现 1.91% 的销售增长。

Conclusion: CoCo 具备模块化、模型无关的设计，适合需要知识增强推理与个性化适配的下一代推荐系统，具备良好扩展性与实际落地潜力。

Abstract: The integration of large language models (LLMs) into recommendation systems
has revealed promising potential through their capacity to extract world
knowledge for enhanced reasoning capabilities. However, current methodologies
that adopt static schema-based prompting mechanisms encounter significant
limitations: (1) they employ universal template structures that neglect the
multi-faceted nature of user preference diversity; (2) they implement
superficial alignment between semantic knowledge representations and behavioral
feature spaces without achieving comprehensive latent space integration. To
address these challenges, we introduce CoCo, an end-to-end framework that
dynamically constructs user-specific contextual knowledge embeddings through a
dual-mechanism approach. Our method realizes profound integration of semantic
and behavioral latent dimensions via adaptive knowledge fusion and
contradiction resolution modules. Experimental evaluations across diverse
benchmark datasets and an enterprise-level e-commerce platform demonstrate
CoCo's superiority, achieving a maximum 8.58% improvement over seven
cutting-edge methods in recommendation accuracy. The framework's deployment on
a production advertising system resulted in a 1.91% sales growth, validating
its practical effectiveness. With its modular design and model-agnostic
architecture, CoCo provides a versatile solution for next-generation
recommendation systems requiring both knowledge-enhanced reasoning and
personalized adaptation.

</details>


### [128] [Large Reasoning Embedding Models: Towards Next-Generation Dense Retrieval Paradigm](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.14321)
*Jianting Tang,Dongshuai Li,Tao Wen,Fuyu Lv,Dan Ou,Linli Xu*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: LREM通过在查询嵌入中引入推理过程来增强密集检索，特别是针对与目标物品存在显著词汇差异的困难查询。通过两阶段训练（先用Query-CoT-Item三元组进行SFT和InfoNCE，再通过RL优化推理轨迹），生成推理增强的查询嵌入以提高召回准确性，并在实际平台上线部署。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于嵌入的密集检索易受对比学习的统计共现偏差影响，难以为含有明显词汇差异的查询提供深层语义匹配，导致检索效果下降。需要将推理能力融入表示学习以桥接查询与商品之间的语义鸿沟。

Method: 提出Large Reasoning Embedding Model (LREM)，对困难查询先进行推理以获得深层理解，再输出推理增强的查询嵌入用于检索；采用两阶段训练：阶段1在精心挑选的Query-CoT-Item三元组上进行SFT和InfoNCE，建立初步推理与嵌入能力；阶段2通过强化学习进一步优化推理轨迹。

Result: 在离线与在线实验中均验证了LREM的有效性，提升检索准确性，且已自2025年8月起部署在中国最大的电商平台上。

Conclusion: 将推理融入嵌入学习可显著缩小原始查询与目标商品之间的语义差距，特别是对困难查询，提升密集检索性能，具备大规模真实场景落地潜力。

Abstract: In modern e-commerce search systems, dense retrieval has become an
indispensable component. By computing similarities between query and item
(product) embeddings, it efficiently selects candidate products from
large-scale repositories. With the breakthroughs in large language models
(LLMs), mainstream embedding models have gradually shifted from BERT to LLMs
for more accurate text modeling. However, these models still adopt
direct-embedding methods, and the semantic accuracy of embeddings remains
inadequate. Therefore, contrastive learning is heavily employed to achieve
tight semantic alignment between positive pairs. Consequently, such models tend
to capture statistical co-occurrence patterns in the training data, biasing
them toward shallow lexical and semantic matches. For difficult queries
exhibiting notable lexical disparity from target items, the performance
degrades significantly. In this work, we propose the Large Reasoning Embedding
Model (LREM), which novelly integrates reasoning processes into representation
learning. For difficult queries, LREM first conducts reasoning to achieve a
deep understanding of the original query, and then produces a
reasoning-augmented query embedding for retrieval. This reasoning process
effectively bridges the semantic gap between original queries and target items,
significantly improving retrieval accuracy. Specifically, we adopt a two-stage
training process: the first stage optimizes the LLM on carefully curated
Query-CoT-Item triplets with SFT and InfoNCE losses to establish preliminary
reasoning and embedding capabilities, and the second stage further refines the
reasoning trajectories via reinforcement learning (RL). Extensive offline and
online experiments validate the effectiveness of LREM, leading to its
deployment on China's largest e-commerce platform since August 2025.

</details>


### [129] [Ensembling Multiple Hallucination Detectors Trained on VLLM Internal Representations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.14330)
*Yuto Nakamizo,Ryuhei Miyazato,Hikaru Tanabe,Ryuta Yamakura,Kiori Hatanaka*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 本文报告团队 y3h2 在 KDD Cup 2025 的 Meta CRAG-MM 挑战中夺得第5名。通过基于逻辑回归的幻觉检测器，利用隐藏状态和注意力头输出，进行模型集成，显著降低VLM幻觉，尽管以牺牲部分正确答案为代价，但提升了鲁棒性；实现细节与代码可在给定链接获取。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在面向图像的视觉问答任务中，尤其是对包含自我中心视角的图像，模型易产生“幻觉”式错误。由于评测采用基于LLM的自动评估并对错误答案给负分，降低内部表示引发的幻觉对提升得分和稳定性至关重要。本研究通过在模型内部表示层面检测并抑制幻觉来提升问答可靠性。

Method: 提出基于逻辑回归的幻觉检测模型，利用VLM的隐藏状态以及特定注意力头的输出作为特征；训练多个检测器并进行集成，以形成稳健的幻觉抑制策略，进而影响VQA的最终输出。

Result: 在竞赛中取得第5名的成绩，显著降低幻觉发生率；为提高鲁棒性而愿意牺牲部分正确性。该方法的实施细节与代码公开在Starter Kit中。

Conclusion: 通过对VLM内部表示的幻觉信号进行检测与集成抑制，可以在对负分制约的VQA评测环境中提升答案的可信度。该思路具有可重复性，但存在准确性与保真度之间的权衡，可进一步通过更强的特征、不同模型家族或后处理策略提升综合表现。

Abstract: This paper presents the 5th place solution by our team, y3h2, for the Meta
CRAG-MM Challenge at KDD Cup 2025. The CRAG-MM benchmark is a visual question
answering (VQA) dataset focused on factual questions about images, including
egocentric images. The competition was contested based on VQA accuracy, as
judged by an LLM-based automatic evaluator. Since incorrect answers result in
negative scores, our strategy focused on reducing hallucinations from the
internal representations of the VLM. Specifically, we trained logistic
regression-based hallucination detection models using both the hidden_state and
the outputs of specific attention heads. We then employed an ensemble of these
models. As a result, while our method sacrificed some correct answers, it
significantly reduced hallucinations and allowed us to place among the top
entries on the final leaderboard. For implementation details and code, please
refer to
https://gitlab.aicrowd.com/htanabe/meta-comprehensive-rag-benchmark-starter-kit.

</details>


### [130] [GemiRec: Interest Quantization and Generation for Multi-Interest Recommendation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.14626)
*Zhibo Wu,Yunfan Wu,Quan Liu,Lin Jiang,Ping Yang,Yao Hu*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: GemiRec introduces a framework for multi-interest recommendation that tackles interest collapse and insufficient evolution modeling via two core ideas: interest quantization for structural separation and interest generation for evolving dynamics, implemented via three modules (IDMM, MIPDM, MIRM). It shows solid theoretical and empirical results and has been deployed in production since March 2025.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Existing multi-interest recommendation methods suffer from two main issues: (1) interest collapse where multiple user representations become homogenized, and (2) poor modeling of interest evolution, missing latent interests not present in historical behavior. A framework-level refinement is proposed to explicitly separate and generate evolving interests.

Method: Propose a three-module framework. (a) Interest Dictionary Maintenance Module (IDMM) maintains a shared, quantized interest dictionary to enforce structural separation of interests. (b) Multi-Interest Posterior Distribution Module (MIPDM) uses a generative model to capture the distribution of future user interests. (c) Multi-Interest Retrieval Module (MIRM) retrieves items using multiple user-interest representations. The framework emphasizes quantization-based separation and generation-based evolution, supported by theoretical and empirical analyses.

Result: The approach demonstrates advantages theoretically and empirically, with extensive experiments validating effectiveness. It has been deployed in production since March 2025, attesting to practical applicability in industry.

Conclusion: GemiRec provides a principled solution to the two core limitations of multi-interest recommendation, enabling better structural separation and evolving interest modeling, with demonstrated effectiveness and industrial deployment.

Abstract: Multi-interest recommendation has gained attention, especially in industrial
retrieval stage. Unlike classical dual-tower methods, it generates multiple
user representations instead of a single one to model comprehensive user
interests. However, prior studies have identified two underlying limitations:
the first is interest collapse, where multiple representations homogenize. The
second is insufficient modeling of interest evolution, as they struggle to
capture latent interests absent from a user's historical behavior. We begin
with a thorough review of existing works in tackling these limitations. Then,
we attempt to tackle these limitations from a new perspective. Specifically, we
propose a framework-level refinement for multi-interest recommendation, named
GemiRec. The proposed framework leverages interest quantization to enforce a
structural interest separation and interest generation to learn the evolving
dynamics of user interests explicitly. It comprises three modules: (a) Interest
Dictionary Maintenance Module (IDMM) maintains a shared quantized interest
dictionary. (b) Multi-Interest Posterior Distribution Module (MIPDM) employs a
generative model to capture the distribution of user future interests. (c)
Multi-Interest Retrieval Module (MIRM) retrieves items using multiple
user-interest representations. Both theoretical and empirical analyses, as well
as extensive experiments, demonstrate its advantages and effectiveness.
Moreover, it has been deployed in production since March 2025, showing its
practical value in industrial applications.

</details>


### [131] [MR.Rec: Synergizing Memory and Reasoning for Personalized Recommendation Assistant with LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.14629)
*Jiani Huang,Xingchen Zou,Lianghao Xia,Qing Li*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 提出 MR.Rec，通过结合动态记忆检索与推理来增强基于LLM的推荐系统，结合RAG与强化学习实现更个性化、可推理的推荐。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前LLM在推荐场景中受限于有限的上下文窗口和单轮推理，难以捕捉动态用户偏好并进行前瞻性推理；需要将记忆与推理结合以实现更深度的个性化。

Method: 提出 MR.Rec 框架：1) 构建高效的检索增强生成（RAG）系统，索引并检索外部记忆以提升个性化能力；2) 将记忆检索与推理融合，进行记忆增强的推理，而不仅仅是基于查询的检索；3) 设计强化学习框架，训练LLM 自动学习记忆利用策略和推理 refine 的策略，以实现动态、自适应的推荐。

Result: 在多项实验中，MR.Rec 显著优于最新的基线方法，证明了动态记忆检索+自适应推理在提升推荐质量上的有效性。

Conclusion: 通过将动态记忆检索与自适应推理结合，MR.Rec 能实现更高的准确性、上下文感知与个性化，并具备扩展潜力；计划公开代码与数据以促进重复性与进一步研究。

Abstract: The application of Large Language Models (LLMs) in recommender systems faces
key challenges in delivering deep personalization and intelligent reasoning,
especially for interactive scenarios. Current methods are often constrained by
limited context windows and single-turn reasoning, hindering their ability to
capture dynamic user preferences and proactively reason over recommendation
contexts. To address these limitations, we propose MR.Rec, a novel framework
that synergizes memory and reasoning for LLM-based recommendations. To achieve
personalization, we develop a comprehensive Retrieval-Augmented Generation
(RAG) system that efficiently indexes and retrieves relevant external memory to
enhance LLM personalization capabilities. Furthermore, to enable the synergy
between memory and reasoning, our RAG system goes beyond conventional
query-based retrieval by integrating reasoning enhanced memory retrieval.
Finally, we design a reinforcement learning framework that trains the LLM to
autonomously learn effective strategies for both memory utilization and
reasoning refinement. By combining dynamic memory retrieval with adaptive
reasoning, this approach ensures more accurate, context-aware, and highly
personalized recommendations. Extensive experiments demonstrate that MR.Rec
significantly outperforms state-of-the-art baselines across multiple metrics,
validating its efficacy in delivering intelligent and personalized
recommendations. We will release code and data upon paper notification.

</details>


### [132] [Causality Enhancement for Cross-Domain Recommendation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.14641)
*Zhibo Wu,Yunfan Wu,Lin Jiang,Ping Yang,Yao Hu*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: CE-CDR 提出一种因果感知的跨域推荐框架：将跨域任务建模成因果图，启发式构建因果感知数据集，推导理论无偏的部分标签因果损失，以泛化至未见跨域模式，并将得到的跨域表示作为插件输入目标域模型，提升目标域推荐；并已于2025年4月在生产中部署。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 跨域推荐中源域任务的不一致性与源特征的因果关系若未被考虑，可能导致信息混杂、负迁移或学习受限。直接使用因果标注数据训练跨域表示虽然理想，但真实场景难以获得无偏的因果标签，因此需要一个可行且广泛适用的因果增强框架来提升跨域效果。

Method: 1) 将跨域推荐重构为一个因果图，以提供 principled 指引；2) 启发式构建因果感知的数据集；3) 推导理论上无偏的 Partial Label Causal Loss，用以从偏置数据泛化到未见跨域模式；4) 产生的跨域表示输入目标模型，作为一个模型无关的插件；5) 进行理论与经验分析及大规模实证；6) 在生产中部署，验证其实用性。

Result: 理论与实验分析验证了 CE-CDR 的合理性与有效性；在多个数据集和真实场景中提升跨域表示与目标域推荐性能，且具有良好的插件属性与泛化能力；自2025年4月起已在生产环境中部署，具备实际落地价值。

Conclusion: CE-CDR 提供了一个通用且模型无关的跨域推荐插件，通过因果化建模、因果感知数据与无偏损失实现对未见跨域模式的有效泛化，能显著提升跨域推荐系统的性能与应用价值。

Abstract: Cross-domain recommendation forms a crucial component in recommendation
systems. It leverages auxiliary information through source domain tasks or
features to enhance target domain recommendations. However, incorporating
inconsistent source domain tasks may result in insufficient cross-domain
modeling or negative transfer. While incorporating source domain features
without considering the underlying causal relationships may limit their
contribution to final predictions. Thus, a natural idea is to directly train a
cross-domain representation on a causality-labeled dataset from the source to
target domain. Yet this direction has been rarely explored, as identifying
unbiased real causal labels is highly challenging in real-world scenarios. In
this work, we attempt to take a first step in this direction by proposing a
causality-enhanced framework, named CE-CDR. Specifically, we first reformulate
the cross-domain recommendation as a causal graph for principled guidance. We
then construct a causality-aware dataset heuristically. Subsequently, we derive
a theoretically unbiased Partial Label Causal Loss to generalize beyond the
biased causality-aware dataset to unseen cross-domain patterns, yielding an
enriched cross-domain representation, which is then fed into the target model
to enhance target-domain recommendations. Theoretical and empirical analyses,
as well as extensive experiments, demonstrate the rationality and effectiveness
of CE-CDR and its general applicability as a model-agnostic plugin. Moreover,
it has been deployed in production since April 2025, showing its practical
value in real-world applications.

</details>


### [133] [Dataset Pruning in RecSys and ML: Best Practice or Mal-Practice?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.14704)
*Leonie Winter*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 数据 pruning 会极大改变数据集特征和算法性能；在剪裁数据上的高性能往往不能泛化到未剪裁数据，且剪裁越严格，测试数据表现越受影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 离线评估严重依赖数据集的特性，需理解数据修剪（ prune）对特征分布、样本量、和算法评估结果的影响，以避免对方法的过度乐观结论。

Method: 对五个基准数据集在未剪裁和五个剪裁级别（5、10、20、50、100）下进行对比分析；对十一种代表算法进行训练与测试；还评估用剪裁训练集在未剪裁测试集上的性能，以检验是否产生虚高效果。

Result: 剪裁极具选择性，有些数据集仅保留原始用户的约2%；在剪裁数据上，传统算法的 ndcg@10 往往提高，但在未剪裁测试集上这一优势基本消失；总体在未剪裁数据上，随剪裁程度增加，算法性能下降，表明数据量减少与分布改变显著影响性能。

Conclusion: 数据修剪会显著改变数据集特征与算法表现，可能引入对方法的过度乐观评估；在进行离线评估时应考虑未剪裁数据、报告修剪级别，并采用更稳健的评估策略以提升可重复性。

Abstract: Offline evaluations in recommender system research depend heavily on
datasets, many of which are pruned, such as the widely used MovieLens
collections. This thesis examines the impact of data pruning - specifically,
removing users with fewer than a specified number of interactions - on both
dataset characteristics and algorithm performance. Five benchmark datasets were
analysed in both their unpruned form and at five successive pruning levels (5,
10, 20, 50, 100). For each coreset, we examined structural and distributional
characteristics and trained and tested eleven representative algorithms. To
further assess if pruned datasets lead to artificially inflated performance
results, we also evaluated models trained on the pruned train sets but tested
on unpruned data. Results show that commonly applied core pruning can be highly
selective, leaving as little as 2% of the original users in some datasets.
Traditional algorithms achieved higher nDCG@10 scores when both training and
testing on pruned data; however, this advantage largely disappeared when
evaluated on unpruned test sets. Across all algorithms, performance declined
with increasing pruning levels when tested on unpruned data, highlighting the
impact of dataset reduction on the performance of recommender algorithms.

</details>


### [134] [Cross-Scenario Unified Modeling of User Interests at Billion Scale](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.14788)
*Manjie Xu,Cheng Chen,Xin Jia,Jingyi Zhou,Yongji Wu,Zejian Wang,Chi Zhang,Kai Zuo,Yibo Chen,Xu Tang,Yao Hu,Yixin Zhu*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: RED-Rec 是一个基于LLM的分层推荐引擎，面向多场景的内容平台，能够在跨场景整合用户兴趣并提升推荐与广告效果，通过两塔结构和场景感知的混合与查询策略实现高效部署和细粒度意图表达；在 RedNote 的在线A/B测试中获得显著性能提升，并引入百万规模的 RED-MMU 序列推荐数据集以支持离线训练与评估。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统推荐系统多在独立场景内优化商业指标，忽视跨场景的行为信号，且在亿级部署中整合大型语言模型（LLMs）困难，难以捕捉跨触点的整体用户兴趣。

Method: 提出 RED-Rec：通过聚合和综合来自搜索、信息流、内容发现等多场景的行为，统一用户兴趣表示；采用两塔结构的 LLM 驱动框架实现多维表征；引入场景感知的密集混合与查询策略，在服务端融合多场景信号并表达细粒度、场景特定的意图。

Result: 在 RedNote 上进行的在线A/B 测试覆盖数亿用户，显示内容推荐和广告投放的显著性能提升；此外提出百万级序列推荐数据集 RED-MMU，用于全面的离线训练与评估。

Conclusion: 推动统一的用户建模，提升个性化深度和大规模UGC平台的用户互动质量。

Abstract: User interests on content platforms are inherently diverse, manifesting
through complex behavioral patterns across heterogeneous scenarios such as
search, feed browsing, and content discovery. Traditional recommendation
systems typically prioritize business metric optimization within isolated
specific scenarios, neglecting cross-scenario behavioral signals and struggling
to integrate advanced techniques like LLMs at billion-scale deployments, which
finally limits their ability to capture holistic user interests across platform
touchpoints. We propose RED-Rec, an LLM-enhanced hierarchical Recommender
Engine for Diversified scenarios, tailored for industry-level content
recommendation systems. RED-Rec unifies user interest representations across
multiple behavioral contexts by aggregating and synthesizing actions from
varied scenarios, resulting in comprehensive item and user modeling. At its
core, a two-tower LLM-powered framework enables nuanced, multifaceted
representations with deployment efficiency, and a scenario-aware dense mixing
and querying policy effectively fuses diverse behavioral signals to capture
cross-scenario user intent patterns and express fine-grained, context-specific
intents during serving. We validate RED-Rec through online A/B testing on
hundreds of millions of users in RedNote through online A/B testing, showing
substantial performance gains in both content recommendation and advertisement
targeting tasks. We further introduce a million-scale sequential recommendation
dataset, RED-MMU, for comprehensive offline training and evaluation. Our work
advances unified user modeling, unlocking deeper personalization and fostering
more meaningful user engagement in large-scale UGC platforms.

</details>


### [135] [A Simulation Framework for Studying Systemic Effects of Feedback Loops in Recommender Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.14857)
*Gabriele Barlacchi,Margherita Lalli,Emanuele Ferragina,Fosca Giannotti,Luca Pappalardo*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 回馈循环在个体层面提升多样性，但削弱整体多样性并强烈集中热卖商品，且可能导致用户偏好趋同。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 揭示长期推荐系统对用户行为和市场结构的影响，评估个性化与长期多样性之间的权衡。

Method: 构建一个仿真框架来在不断演化的用户-商品交互上定期重新训练推荐器，并使用亚马逊电商数据集分析不同算法对多样性、购买集中度和用户同质化的影响。

Result: 发现存在系统性权衡：反馈循环可能增加个体层面的多样性，但同时降低群体层面的多样性，并使对少数热门商品的需求集中；在某些系统中，反馈循环也提高了用户购买档案的相似性。

Conclusion: 需要设计在提高个性化的同时兼顾长期多样性和市场健康的推荐策略，防止长期的多样性下降和用户同质化。

Abstract: Recommender systems continuously interact with users, creating feedback loops
that shape both individual behavior and collective market dynamics. This paper
introduces a simulation framework to model these loops in online retail
environments, where recommenders are periodically retrained on evolving
user-item interactions. Using the Amazon e-Commerce dataset, we analyze how
different recommendation algorithms influence diversity, purchase
concentration, and user homogenization over time. Results reveal a systematic
trade-off: while the feedback loop increases individual diversity, it
simultaneously reduces collective diversity and concentrates demand on a few
popular items. Moreover, for some recommender systems, the feedback loop
increases user homogenization over time, making user purchase profiles
increasingly similar. These findings underscore the need for recommender
designs that balance personalization with long-term diversity.

to distill into smaller models as proof-of-concepts. Our ultimate aim is to
support retrieval at all scales, from large-scale retrieval which lives in the
cloud to models that can run locally, on any device. mxbai-edge-colbert-v0 is a
model that we hope will serve as a solid foundation backbone for all future
experiments, representing the first version of a long series of small
proof-of-concepts. As part of the development of mxbai-edge-colbert-v0, we
conducted multiple ablation studies, of which we report the results. In terms
of downstream performance, mxbai-edge-colbert-v0 is a particularly capable
small model, outperforming ColBERTv2 on common short-text benchmarks (BEIR) and
representing a large step forward in long-context tasks, with unprecedented
efficiency.

### [137] [Large Language Models for Real-World IoT Device Identification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.13817)
*Rameen Mahmood,Tousif Ahmed,Sai Teja Peddinti,Danny Yuxing Huang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 将设备识别视为语言建模任务，通过对异构网络元数据进行语义推断来实现高精度的IoT设备识别，具有鲁棒性和可扩展性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: IoT设备规模快速膨胀使现有识别方法跟不上，开放世界中的元数据往往缺失、噪声化或被对抗性篡改，因此需要一个可扩展、可解释且对噪声与缺失鲁棒的识别框架。

Method: 构建语义推断流水线，将识别任务转化为语言模型任务；通过互信息与熵稳定性分数，利用多模态大语言模型对IoT Inspector数据集生成高保真厂商标签；对量化的LLaMA3.18B进行指令微调，采用课程学习以提升对稀疏分布和长尾厂商的泛化。

Result: 在2,015个厂商上达到98.25% Top-1准确率和90.73%宏观准确率；对缺失字段、协议漂移和对抗操控具有鲁棒性；在独立测试平台及解释质量、对抗压力测试中表现良好，显示指令微调的LLM在真实大规模场景下具备可扩展性与可解释性。

Conclusion: 将指令微调的LLM作为可扩展、可解释的设备识别基础，适用于大规模现实场景，并在开放世界环境提供更强的安全性与隐私保障。

Abstract: The rapid expansion of IoT devices has outpaced current identification
methods, creating significant risks for security, privacy, and network
accountability. These challenges are heightened in open-world environments,
where traffic metadata is often incomplete, noisy, or intentionally obfuscated.
We introduce a semantic inference pipeline that reframes device identification
as a language modeling task over heterogeneous network metadata. To construct
reliable supervision, we generate high-fidelity vendor labels for the IoT
Inspector dataset, the largest real-world IoT traffic corpus, using an ensemble
of large language models guided by mutual-information and entropy-based
stability scores. We then instruction-tune a quantized LLaMA3.18B model with
curriculum learning to support generalization under sparsity and long-tail
vendor distributions. Our model achieves 98.25% top-1 accuracy and 90.73% macro
accuracy across 2,015 vendors while maintaining resilience to missing fields,
protocol drift, and adversarial manipulation. Evaluation on an independent IoT
testbed, coupled with explanation quality and adversarial stress tests,
demonstrates that instruction-tuned LLMs provide a scalable and interpretable
foundation for real-world device identification at scale.

### [138] [Self-Training with Dynamic Weighting for Robust Gradual Domain Adaptation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.13864)
*Zixi Wang,Yushe Cao,Yubo Huang,Jinzhu Wei,Jingzehua Xu,Shuai Zhang,Xin Lai*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出了一种带动态权重的自训练方法 STDW，用于逐步域自适应，动态调节源/目标损失权重，并通过伪标签和自训练实现平滑知识迁移，在多数据集上优于 baselines，关键在于参数 ρ 的动态调度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在源域到目标域存在平滑迁移的挑战，传统逐步域自适应受限于中间数据不足或知识迁移不充分，需更稳健的自训练框架。

Method: 提出带动态权重的自训练框架，使用随时间变化的超参数 ρ 从 0 到 1 控制源/目标域学习强度，利用自训练产生伪标签并优化加权目标函数，结合中间域以实现渐进适应。

Result: 在 rotated MNIST、color-shifted MNIST、portrait 数据集及 Cover Type 上表现优于 baselines；消融显示 ρ 的动态调度对减少域偏移和提升泛化重要。

Conclusion: 给出理论洞见与实用框架，适用于动态现实场景；代码公开。

Abstract: In this paper, we propose a new method called Self-Training with Dynamic
Weighting (STDW), which aims to enhance robustness in Gradual Domain Adaptation
(GDA) by addressing the challenge of smooth knowledge migration from the source
to the target domain. Traditional GDA methods mitigate domain shift through
intermediate domains and self-training but often suffer from inefficient
knowledge migration or incomplete intermediate data. Our approach introduces a
dynamic weighting mechanism that adaptively balances the loss contributions of
the source and target domains during training. Specifically, we design an
optimization framework governed by a time-varying hyperparameter $\varrho$
(progressing from 0 to 1), which controls the strength of domain-specific
learning and ensures stable adaptation. The method leverages self-training to
generate pseudo-labels and optimizes a weighted objective function for
iterative model updates, maintaining robustness across intermediate domains.
Experiments on rotated MNIST, color-shifted MNIST, portrait datasets, and the
Cover Type dataset demonstrate that STDW outperforms existing baselines.
Ablation studies further validate the critical role of $\varrho$'s dynamic
scheduling in achieving progressive adaptation, confirming its effectiveness in
reducing domain bias and improving generalization. This work provides both
theoretical insights and a practical framework for robust gradual domain
adaptation, with potential applications in dynamic real-world scenarios. The
code is available at https://github.com/Dramwig/STDW.

</details>


### [139] [Deep Edge Filter: Return of the Human-Crafted Layer in Deep Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.13865)
*Dongkwan Lee,Junhoo Lee,Nojun Kwak*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出 Deep Edge Filter，通过对深层特征进行高通滤波以去除低频域偏差，从而提取更具泛化性的表示，在 Vision、文本、3D、音频等多模态任务上实现稳定提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 假设高频分量携带任务相关语义，低频分量包含域特定偏差；对比低通输出与原始特征以得到更通用的表示。

Method: 对深层网络特征进行低通滤波后再与原始特征相减，得到高频分量，保持网络架构不变；实现简单，适用于各种模型和模态。

Result: 跨领域、多模态和不同模型架构上均获得性能提升；分析显示特征稀疏化、有效隔离高频分量，验证核心假设。

Conclusion: 该策略提供一种简单且效用强的泛化提升方法，跨域适用性良好，代码可用。

Abstract: We introduce the Deep Edge Filter, a novel approach that applies high-pass
filtering to deep neural network features to improve model generalizability.
Our method is motivated by our hypothesis that neural networks encode
task-relevant semantic information in high-frequency components while storing
domain-specific biases in low-frequency components of deep features. By
subtracting low-pass filtered outputs from original features, our approach
isolates generalizable representations while preserving architectural
integrity. Experimental results across diverse domains such as Vision, Text,
3D, and Audio demonstrate consistent performance improvements regardless of
model architecture and data modality. Analysis reveals that our method induces
feature sparsification and effectively isolates high-frequency components,
providing empirical validation of our core hypothesis. The code is available at
https://github.com/dongkwani/DeepEdgeFilter.

### [140] [CoLoR-GAN: Continual Few-Shot Learning with Low-Rank Adaptation in Generative Adversarial Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.13869)
*Munsif Ali,Leonardo Rossi,Massimo Bertozzi*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出 CoLoR-GAN，通过低秩张量和 LoRA 系列方法实现对生成对抗网络的持续学习与少样本适应，降低参数量同时达到SOTA。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在生成对抗网络的持续学习场景中，少样本学习易产生灾难性忘记；现有方法如 LFS-GAN 引入大量新权重，长期训练成本高，需更高效的参数利用方案。

Method: 提出 CoLoR-GAN 框架，结合低秩张量的适配与 LoRA，卷积层引入 LoRA，并提出 LoRA-in-LoRA（LLoRA）以进一步紧凑化；对超参数进行经验性分析。

Result: 在若干基准CL和FS任务上表现出SOTA性能，同时参数规模显著降低，源代码公开。

Conclusion: 将低秩适配和LoRA用于持续学习的GANs具备有效性与高效性，LLoRA 进一步提升压缩效果，并提供便于选择超参数的实验趋势。

Abstract: Continual learning (CL) in the context of Generative Adversarial Networks
(GANs) remains a challenging problem, particularly when it comes to learn from
a few-shot (FS) samples without catastrophic forgetting. Current most effective
state-of-the-art (SOTA) methods, like LFS-GAN, introduce a non-negligible
quantity of new weights at each training iteration, which would become
significant when considering the long term. For this reason, this paper
introduces \textcolor{red}{\textbf{\underline{c}}}ontinual
few-sh\textcolor{red}{\textbf{\underline{o}}}t learning with
\textcolor{red}{\textbf{\underline{lo}}}w-\textcolor{red}{\textbf{\underline{r}}}ank
adaptation in GANs named CoLoR-GAN, a framework designed to handle both FS and
CL together, leveraging low-rank tensors to efficiently adapt the model to
target tasks while reducing even more the number of parameters required.
Applying a vanilla LoRA implementation already permitted us to obtain pretty
good results. In order to optimize even further the size of the adapters, we
challenged LoRA limits introducing a LoRA in LoRA (LLoRA) technique for
convolutional layers. Finally, aware of the criticality linked to the choice of
the hyperparameters of LoRA, we provide an empirical study to easily find the
best ones. We demonstrate the effectiveness of CoLoR-GAN through experiments on
several benchmark CL and FS tasks and show that our model is efficient,
reaching SOTA performance but with a number of resources enormously reduced.
Source code is available on
\href{https://github.com/munsifali11/CoLoR-GAN}{Github.

</details>


### [141] [Joint Discriminative-Generative Modeling via Dual Adversarial Training](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.13872)
*Xuwang Yin,Claire Zhang,Julie Steele,Nir Shavit,Tony T. Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出一个基于对抗性训练的能量模型框架，替换SGLD的JEM训练，以实现鲁棒分类和高保真生成的统一方法。在ImageNet等数据集上，生成效果超越BigGAN并接近扩散模型，证明了基于MCMC的EBM在高分辨率数据上的生成能力，同时显著提升对抗鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决混合模型（如JEM）在训练中的不稳定性和样本质量差问题，寻求一个统一框架同时提高分类鲁棒性与生成保真度。

Method: 核心创新包括：(1) 用基于对抗训练的能量函数学习替代SGLD的JEM，通过对真实数据与PGD生成的对比样本进行二元交叉熵（BCE）训练来优化能量函数；(2) 协同对抗训练以提升判别鲁棒性，且不需要显式梯度惩罚；(3) 两阶段训练以解决批归一化与EBM训练的不兼容性；在CIFAR-10/100和ImageNet上进行评估，展示能量模型在生成与分类上的双赢。

Result: 相比现有混合模型，显著提升对抗鲁棒性；在生成方面保持竞争力；在ImageNet优化生成时，生成保真度超过BigGAN并接近扩散模型，首次实现了高质量生成的基于MCMC的EBM在复杂高分辨率数据集上的表现。

Conclusion: 证明对抗训练可以成为统一框架的有效基础，使基于EBM的生成与鲁棒分类在同一模型中协同实现，同时通过两阶段训练和无显式梯度惩罚等设计解决了JEM扩展中的稳定性问题。

Abstract: Simultaneously achieving robust classification and high-fidelity generative
modeling within a single framework presents a significant challenge. Hybrid
approaches, such as Joint Energy-Based Models (JEM), interpret classifiers as
EBMs but are often limited by the instability and poor sample quality inherent
in SGLD-based training. We address these limitations by proposing a novel
training framework that integrates adversarial training (AT) principles for
both discriminative robustness and stable generative learning. The proposed
method introduces three key innovations: (1) the replacement of SGLD-based JEM
learning with a stable, AT-based approach that optimizes the energy function by
discriminating between real data and PGD-generated contrastive samples using
the BCE loss; (2) synergistic adversarial training for the discriminative
component that enhances classification robustness while eliminating the need
for explicit gradient penalties; and (3) a two-stage training procedure to
resolve the incompatibility between batch normalization and EBM training.
Experiments on CIFAR-10, CIFAR-100, and ImageNet demonstrate that our method
substantially improves adversarial robustness over existing hybrid models while
maintaining competitive generative performance. On ImageNet, when optimized for
generative modeling, our model's generative fidelity surpasses that of BigGAN
and approaches diffusion models, representing the first MCMC-based EBM approach
to achieve high-quality generation on complex, high-resolution datasets. Our
approach addresses key stability issues that have limited JEM scaling and
demonstrates that adversarial training can serve as an effective foundation for
unified frameworks capable of generating and robustly classifying visual data.

</details>


### [142] [K-frames: Scene-Driven Any-k Keyframe Selection for long video understanding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.13891)

Abstract: Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs) have demonstrated significant

approach, we first introduce PeakClips, a dataset of 200K video highlights

### [143] [Multi-View Semi-Supervised Label Distribution Learning with Local Structure Complementarity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.13917)
*Yanshan Xiao,Kaihong Wu,Bo Liu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出了 MVSS-LDL：多视角半监督标签分布学习，通过利用每个视图的局部最近邻结构并在视图之间互补，提升标签分布的学习性能，优于单视角方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有 LDL 研究多集中在单视角、有标注数据的场景，缺乏对多视角与半监督信息的充分挖掘。引入多视角信息的互补局部结构可更全面地刻画样本关系，有望提升标签分布的预测能力。

Method: 对于每个视图 v，计算前 k 个最近邻集合；通过将样本 i 在其他视图中的最近邻信息补充到视图 v 的最近邻集合中，得到补充后的局部结构。基于这些补充后的近邻集合，构建图学习基的多视图半监督 LDL 模型，利用各视图之间的互补性来共同学习标签分布。

Result: 数值实验表明，该 MVSS-LDL 相较现有的单视角 LDL 方法在分类性能上有显著提升。

Conclusion: 首次尝试将多视角与半监督 LDL 融合，通过局部结构互补性实现信息互通，取得了明显的性能提升；为未来进一步扩展到更多视图和更复杂的局部结构提供了方向。

Abstract: Label distribution learning (LDL) is a paradigm that each sample is
associated with a label distribution. At present, the existing approaches are
proposed for the single-view LDL problem with labeled data, while the
multi-view LDL problem with labeled and unlabeled data has not been considered.
In this paper, we put forward the multi-view semi-supervised label distribution
learning with local structure complementarity (MVSS-LDL) approach, which
exploits the local nearest neighbor structure of each view and emphasizes the
complementarity of local nearest neighbor structures in multiple views.
Specifically speaking, we first explore the local structure of view $v$ by
computing the $k$-nearest neighbors. As a result, the $k$-nearest neighbor set
of each sample $\boldsymbol{x}_i$ in view $v$ is attained. Nevertheless, this
$k$-nearest neighbor set describes only a part of the nearest neighbor
information of sample $\boldsymbol{x}_i$. In order to obtain a more
comprehensive description of sample $\boldsymbol{x}_i$'s nearest neighbors, we
complement the nearest neighbor set in view $v$ by incorporating sample
$\boldsymbol{x}_i$'s nearest neighbors in other views. Lastly, based on the
complemented nearest neighbor set in each view, a graph learning-based
multi-view semi-supervised LDL model is constructed. By considering the
complementarity of local nearest neighbor structures, different views can
mutually provide the local structural information to complement each other. To
the best of our knowledge, this is the first attempt at multi-view LDL.
Numerical studies have demonstrated that MVSS-LDL attains explicitly better
classification performance than the existing single-view LDL methods.

</details>


### [144] [Weight Weaving: Parameter Pooling for Data-Free Model Merging](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.13921)
*Levy Chaves,Eduardo Valle,Sandra Avila*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决在数据不可访问的情况下设定全局或局部权重系数λ的问题，避免使用评估集的优先数据进行调参，提升模型融合的可用性和数据效率。

Method: 引入Weight Weaving，作为一种即插即用的权重池化策略，通过对λ取值空间进行池化（如平均、随机选择或并现有融合方法）实现对权重的组合。它独立于具体的融合算法，且不需要评估数据。

Result: 在三个ViT变体、三个实验设定（视觉多任务学习、视觉连续学习、领域泛化）中，能普遍改善多种模型融合方法的性能，数据无关设置下平均提升可达15.9个百分点。

Abstract: Model merging provides a cost-effective and data-efficient combination of
specialized deep neural networks through parameter integration. This technique
leverages expert models across downstream tasks without requiring retraining.
Most model merging approaches critically depend on scaling hyper-parameters
$\lambda$, which weight each model's contribution globally or individually.
Principled approaches for setting scaling factors without accessing any data
(data-free) are scarce, often leading researchers to tune $\lambda$ using
privileged data from the evaluation set, which is obviously unfeasible in
practice. To address this limitation, we introduce Weight Weaving, a
plug-and-play technique that pools model weights across $\lambda$ values search
space using user-defined pooling functions, such as averaging, random
selection, or even existing model merging methods. Our method demonstrates high
modularity, imposing minimal constraints on the search space. It operates
orthogonally to existing model merging methods and eliminates evaluation data
requirements. We validate Weight Weaving across three ViT variants in three
experimental setups: vision multi-task learning, vision continual learning, and
domain generalization. Our method consistently improves the performance of
several model merging methods, achieving average accuracy gains of up to 15.9
percentage points in a data-free setting.

### [146] [Distributional Consistency Loss: Beyond Pointwise Data Terms in Inverse Problems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.13972)
*George Webber,Andrew J. Reader*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出分布一致性（DC）损失，用于逆问题的数据一致性评估，通过对每个测量的模型概率分数进行分布层级校准，避免点对点噪声拟合，提升去噪与重建性能；在图像去噪和Poisson噪声医学成像中显示显著优势。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的数据一致性通常采用均方误差或负对数似然进行点对点匹配，易对噪声过拟合且忽略噪声分布信息。若能够利用已知的测量噪声分布与大量独立观测值进行分布层级校准，理论与实践上的鲁棒性可提升。

Method: 提出分布一致性（DC）损失，使用基于模型的概率分数对每个测量进行统计一致性评估，并在数据一致性层面以分布级别进行校准。DC损失可直接替换传统数据一致性项，兼容现有正则化器，使用与传统损失相同的优化方式进行训练，并在不依赖先验的情况下减少对噪声的过拟合。该方法适用于噪声分布已知且测量值独立的场景。

Result: 在两大应用中取得提升：1) 图像去噪中以深度图像先验为基础，使用DC替代MSE后无需早停且PSNR提高；2) Poisson噪声的医学成像重建中，DC降低了高迭代重建的伪影，并提升了手工正则化的效果。

Conclusion: DC损失为逆问题中的一种统计学上有据可依、性能更优的替代数据一致性项的工具，适用于噪声分布已知且观测值多且独立的场景，便于与现有正则化技术结合并提升整体重建性能。

Abstract: Recovering true signals from noisy measurements is a central challenge in
inverse problems spanning medical imaging, geophysics, and signal processing.
Current solutions balance prior assumptions regarding the true signal
(regularization) with agreement to noisy measured data (data-fidelity).
Conventional data-fidelity loss functions, such as mean-squared error (MSE) or
negative log-likelihood, seek pointwise agreement with noisy measurements,
often leading to overfitting to noise. In this work, we instead evaluate
data-fidelity collectively by testing whether the observed measurements are
statistically consistent with the noise distributions implied by the current
estimate. We adopt this aggregated perspective and introduce distributional
consistency (DC) loss, a data-fidelity objective that replaces pointwise
matching with distribution-level calibration using model-based probability
scores for each measurement. DC loss acts as a direct and practical plug-in
replacement for standard data consistency terms: i) it is compatible with
modern regularizers, ii) it is optimized in the same way as traditional losses,
and iii) it avoids overfitting to measurement noise even without the use of
priors. Its scope naturally fits many practical inverse problems where the
measurement-noise distribution is known and where the measured dataset consists
of many independent noisy values. We demonstrate efficacy in two key example
application areas: i) in image denoising with deep image prior, using DC
instead of MSE loss removes the need for early stopping and achieves higher
PSNR; ii) in medical image reconstruction from Poisson-noisy data, DC loss
reduces artifacts in highly-iterated reconstructions and enhances the efficacy
of hand-crafted regularization. These results position DC loss as a
statistically grounded, performance-enhancing alternative to conventional
fidelity losses for inverse problems.

*Xun Wu,Shaohan Huang,Wenhui Wang,Ting Song,Li Dong,Yan Xia,Furu Wei*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决大模型在特定任务上的高内存与推理成本问题；现有低精度微调存在性能差距，需有效方法缩小与全精度模型的差距；提出一个可在现成 LLM 上实现低成本高效微调的方案。

Method: 提出三大核心技术：1) SubLN 模块（来自 BitNet）用于轻量化的层归一化/权重处理；2) 基于 MiniLM 的多头自注意力蒸馏；3) 持续预训练作为热身步骤，缓解 1.58-bit 与 FP 微调在特定任务上的性能缺口的放大问题。

Result: 在不同模型规模上，BitDistill 的任务性能接近全精度对等模型；实现可观的内存节省（最高 10x）和 CPU 推理加速（约 2.65x）。

Abstract: In this paper, we present BitNet Distillation (BitDistill), a lightweight
pipeline that fine-tunes off-the-shelf full-precision LLMs (e.g., Qwen) into
1.58-bit precision (i.e., ternary weights {-1, 0, 1}) for specific downstream
tasks, achieving strong task-specific performance with minimal computational
cost. Specifically, BitDistill incorporates three key techniques: the SubLN
module, as introduced in BitNet; multi-head attention distillation, based on
MiniLM; and continual pre-training, which serves as a crucial warm-up step to
mitigate the scalability issue of the performance gap between finetuned
full-precision and 1.58-bit LLMs on specific tasks. Experimental results show
that BitDistill achieves performance comparable to the full-precision
counterpart models across model size, while enabling up to 10x memory savings
and 2.65x faster inference on CPUs. Code is available at
https://github.com/microsoft/BitNet.
